                                    9708              *        not greater than R1 from the list 1.000, .500, .200, .100,

                                   20825              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20826              Ÿ  CHARCHK/CHARCHKA -- Routine to check string for valid alpha-       Ÿ
                                   20827              Ÿ    numeric characters.  "CHARCHKA" entry is used when the first     Ÿ
                                   20828              Ÿ    character must be alphabetic.                                    Ÿ
                                   20829              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20830              Ÿ      On entry:                                                      Ÿ
                                   20831              Ÿ        R1,R0 - string loc, len                                      Ÿ
                                   20832              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20833              Ÿ      On exit, R15 (and CC):                                         Ÿ
                                   20834              Ÿ        -4 - national chars (@,#,$) present                          Ÿ
                                   20835              Ÿ         0 - all chars ok                                            Ÿ
                                   20836              Ÿ         4 - invalid string                                          Ÿ
                                   20837              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20838              Ÿ  Usage notes:                                                       Ÿ
                                   20839              Ÿ  CHARCHK has only 1 caller. It is used to check JES ID jobname      Ÿ
                                   20840              Ÿ  option.  CHARCHKA is tested as follows, BNZ is used for a          Ÿ
                                   20841              Ÿ  ALpha followed by alphanumerics.  BP (error routine) is used       Ÿ
                                   20842              Ÿ  to check for valid JCL jobnames (ie nationals and alphas           Ÿ
                                   20843              Ÿ  are treated the same).  It might be clearer to change as           Ÿ
                                   20844              Ÿ  suggested below in the TO DO: comments.                            Ÿ
                                   20845              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20846              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20847              Ÿ  Note:                                                              Ÿ
                                   20848              Ÿ  Characters are not checked for case.  They may be in               Ÿ
                                   20849              Ÿ  upper, lower or mixed case.  If you want upper case,               Ÿ
                                   20850              Ÿ  then be sure the translation to upper case is done by              Ÿ
                                   20851              Ÿ  the calling routine.                                               Ÿ
                                   20852              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20853              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20854              Ÿ  To Do:                                                             Ÿ
                                   20855              Ÿ  Should make 3 routines:                                            Ÿ
                                   20856              Ÿ  CHARCHKA - Alpha 1st char, then alphanumerics, no nationals        Ÿ
                                   20857              Ÿ  CHARCHKB - Alpha 1st char, then alphanumerics, with                Ÿ
                                   20858              Ÿ   nationals the same as alphas. (B for Batch job names)             Ÿ
                                   20859              Ÿ  CHARCHK - alpha numeric or national                                Ÿ
                                   20860              Ÿ  The ACMD,JES,RJE call CHARCHKB (batch).                            Ÿ
                                   20861              Ÿ  the DOPT,OPT,EDIT call CHARCHKA.                                   Ÿ
                                   20862              Ÿ  With the above strategy, we only chech Z,NZ after call.            Ÿ
